Restaurant: The hotel has a wide variety of breakfast options, but it seems to be too early to end at 10 o'clock, so after 9:15, there will be many people like a street market. Staff service is very fast and professional.

I told the waitress and she gave me a new one immediately, which is worthy of praise. The air-conditioning in the hotel room is not enough, and I can't sleep if it gets hotter. The hotel's bathtub is large and comfortable, but it is not balanced. Please ask the hotel to find workers to make repairs. Check-in: The staff is fairly professional, but it would be better if they can take the initiative and smile. Feels like a 4 star hotel quality. However, the decoration and style of the hotel lobby is not bad. In addition, we found that someone was secretly smoking in the corridor, and hoped to do a good job of checking it early (personal reason: because once I smell the smell of smoke, I will feel uncomfortable for the next one to two hours); the smell of the hotel corridor is fresh, tidy.

Conclusion: Generally speaking, this hotel is also at a five-star level. If the above things can be improved, it will definitely be more popular. I am also interested in trying to stay again in the future.

High-quality staff: FO Chaya (after making coffee for us, asked us about our living experience intimately, which is worthy of praise), Auntie Procter & Gamble on the 8th floor (when we have extra needs, her service is very good, she is also very polite and sincere smile)
